Manual model testing#

This notebook contains a number of tests for the simulation model where the output must be interpreted by a user to determine if the model is functioning correctly. This may include inspecting:

  • a simulated log of events

  • the distribution of an output

  • a chart or plot produced by the model

Imports#

import numpy as np
import simpy

Model code imports#

from ccu_formatted_code_stage2 import *

Tests#

Constants and utility functions#

# The extreme value
M = 10_000_000

def run_test(experiment):
    # Create a SimPy environment
    env = simpy.Environment()
    ccu_model = CCU(env, experiment)
    try:
        results = ccu_model.run()
    except ZeroDivisionError:
        results = None
    
    return ccu_model, results

def test_extreme_value_only_ed(extreme_value=M*5):
    '''
    Extreme value test 1: 
    
    Wards, Em Surgery, other hospitals, x-ray, electives have their inter-arrival time
    set to $M$ a very large number.
    
    Expected result: 
    ----------------
    The only type of patient to arrive to the model is "Accident and Emergency."
    Seen in trace.

    See also automatic test version:
   
    Quantitative: There are no elective cancellations (as no electives arrive)
    '''
    experiment = Experiment(wards_arrival_rate = extreme_value,
                            emergency_surgery_arrival_rate = extreme_value, other_hospitals_arrival_rate = extreme_value,
                            xray_department_arrival_rate = extreme_value, elective_surgery_arrival_rate = extreme_value,
                            trace=True, results_collection_period=200)
    return  run_test(experiment)

_ = test_extreme_value_only_ed()

Extreme value test 2#

Block all arrivals apart from electives

def test_extreme_value_no_unplanned(extreme_value=M*5):
    '''
    Extreme value test 2: 
    
    All unplanned admissions have their inter-arrival time
    set to $M$ a very large number
    
    Expected result: The only type of patient to arrive to the model is "Elective"
    '''
    experiment = Experiment(accident_emergency_arrival_rate = extreme_value, wards_arrival_rate = extreme_value,
                            emergency_surgery_arrival_rate = extreme_value, other_hospitals_arrival_rate = extreme_value,
                            xray_department_arrival_rate = extreme_value, trace=True, results_collection_period=200)
    return run_test(experiment)

_ = test_extreme_value_no_unplanned()

Extreme value test 3#

Critical care beds set to 1.

def test_extreme_value_1_bed(random_number_set=0, trace=False):
    '''
    Extreme value test 3: 
    
    Critical care beds set to 1 or parameter
    
    Expected result: 
    ---------------
    When critical_care_beds=1 queues form after first arrival.
    Cancellations also begin after 1st arrival.
 
    Note: 
    ----
    [1] reported utilisation will typically be near to 100% because of the patient still
    in service.  Small chance > 100 as calculation includes patients 
    
    '''
    experiment = Experiment(num_critical_care_beds=1, 
                            random_number_set=random_number_set,
                            trace=trace)
    model, results = run_test(experiment)
    print(f'{model.total_treatment_time=}')
    print(f'{experiment.results_collection_period=}')
    return model, results

The first run examines the trace. We expect that after the first arrival Elective cancellations begin and unplanned admissions begin to wait.

_ = test_extreme_value_1_bed(trace=True)

model.total_treatment_time=7457.194345913006
experiment.results_collection_period=8640

Extreme value test: infinite length of stay#

def extreme_value_test_infinite_los(extreme_value=M, capacity=2):
    '''
    Extreme value test: the means of stay_distributions are set to $M$ 
    a very large number.

    Params:
    -------
    extreme_value: int, optional (default=M)
        The extreme length of stay mean

    capacity: int, optional (default=2)
        The capacity of the unit.
    
    Expected result: 
    ----------------
    After `capacity` arrivals queues form and no patients are admitted.
    '''
    experiment = Experiment(accident_emergency_lognormal_mu=M, 
                 wards_lognormal_mu=M, 
                 emergency_surgery_lognormal_mu=M, 
                 other_hospitals_lognormal_mu=M, 
                 xray_department_lognormal_mu=M, 
                 elective_surgery_treatment_rate=M,
                 num_critical_care_beds=capacity,
                            warm_up_period=0,
                 trace=True)
    
    return run_test(experiment)

_ = extreme_value_test_infinite_los(capacity=24)
